secondly maye doubted whether ionadab well bidding forbeare wine vſe tillage plante vine dwell houſes therein ſemeth ſome great superſtition forbid people god vſe creature thoſe trade life haue iuſte tirannicall oppreſſions chaldee ſuſtained yet nothing moued repent turne frō wickednes wherfore ſome elder thē retaining ſtill heartes onely inclination earneſt affection continue idolatry deſirous vnto touching hope reſtoring hieruſalem forſomuch prophete might haue ben deceiued hipocriſie haue thought truely ſincerely repented god openeth diſſimulation vnto teacheth home ſhall anſwere morning prayer ezechiel 16 agayne worde lorde came vnto ſaying 2 thou ſonne man ſhewe hieruſalem abhominations 3 ſay thus ſayth lord god vnto hieruſalem thy habitation kinred land chanaan thy father amorite thy mother hithite 4 day thy birth thou waſt borne ſtring thy nauell cut thou waſt bathed water make thée clean thou waſt ſalted ſalt ſwadled cloutes 5 eye pitied thée doe theſe thing thée haue compaſſion vpon thée thou waſt vtterly caſt vpon field contempt thy perſon daye thy birth 6 came thée ſaw thée defiled thyne owne bloud ſayd vnto thée thou waſt thy bloud liue euen thou waſt thy bloud ſayd vnto thée liue 7 cauſed thée multiplie bud fielde thou arte growne vp waxen greate thou haſte gotten maruelous pleaſant beautie thy breaſtes faſhioned thy heare goodly growne wheras thou waſt naked bare 8 nowe wente thée looked vpon thée behold thy tyme come yea euen tyme woe thée ſpred cloathes ouer thée couer thy diſhoneſtie yea made othe vnto thée contracted ſelfe thée ſayth lord god ſo thou becameſt myne 9 waſhed thée water purged thy bloud thée anoynted thée oyle 10 cloathed thée broydred woorke ſhod thée badger ſkinne girded thée aboute fine linnen couered thée ſilke 11 decked thée coſtely apparell put bracelet vpon thy handes chayne aboute thy neck 12 put frontlet vpon thy face earerings vpon thyne eares beautiful crowne vpon thine head 13 thus waſt thou deckt golde ſiluer thy rayment fyne linnen ſilke broydred work thou didſt eate fine floure hony oyle maruelous beautifull waſte thou thou didſt luckily proſper kingdome 14 thy name ſpread among heathen thy beautie perfect beautie put vpon thée ſayth lord god 15 thou haſt put thy confidence thyne owne beautie played harlot bicauſe thy renoune haſte poured thy fornication euery one wente thou waſt 16 thou didſt take thy garment deckt thy hie place diuers colour played harlot thervpon come ſhall 17 goodly iewels gaue thée myne owne gold ſiluer haſt thou taken made thée men image therof cōmitmitted whoordome 18 thy broydred garmentes haſt thou taken deckt therewith myne oyle incenſe haſt thou ſet 19 meat gaue thée fine floure oyle honie féede thée withall haſt thou ſet ſwéet ſauour thus ſaith lord god 20 thou haſt taken thine ſonnes daughter thou haſt begotten vnto theſe haſt thou offred vp vnto deuoured ſmall whoordome thineleuit 20 2 leui 18 c 12 2 23 b 6 21 thou haſt ſlaine child deliuered cauſe paſſe thorough fire 22 yet al thine abhominations whoordomes thou haſt remembred dayes thy youth howe naked bare thou waſt time waſt defyled thyne owne bloud 23 theſe thy wickedneſſes wo wo vnto thée ſayth lorde god 24 thou haſte buylte vnto thée hye place haſte made thée hye place euery ſtréete 25 thou haſte buylt thine hie place euery head waye thou haſte made thy beautie abhorred thou haſt opened thy feete euery one came multiplied thy whoordome 26 thou haſt committed fornication egyptian thy neyghbours whiche great fleſhe thus haſt thou increaſed thyne whoordome vnto chaldées yet thou waſt ſatiſfied herewith 30 weake thine heart ſayth lord god ſéeing thou doeſt theſe euen workes preſumptuous whooriſhe woman 31 buylding thy hye place heade euery waye makeſt thy hye place euery ſtréete thou haſte ben whoore holdeth ſcorne rewarde 32 wyfe breaketh wedlocke taketh ſtead hir huſband 33 giftes giuen al whoores thou giueſt rewardes vnto al thy louers rewardeſt come vnto thée euery ſide thy fornication 34 come paſſe thée thy whoordomes contrary vſe woman yea hath ſuche fornication ben committed thée ſéeing thou giueſt giftes vnto reward giuē thée therfore thou art contrarie 35 therfore heare word lord thou harlot 36 thus ſayth lord god bicauſe thou haſte poured thy braſſe diſcouered thy filthines thy fornication thy louers idol thine abhominations
